(1 + $1)/e;\n                # O_EXCL is required for security reasons.\n                sysopen $fh, $base_name, O_WRONLY|O_EXCL|O_CREAT;\n            }\n\n            if( defined fileno($fh) ) {\n                return ($fh, $base_name);\n            }\n            else {\n                return ();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n')
